=== Test/Eval/HYPHEN_MINUS_in_localName

encodingtest.TripleStatementList{
	{
		Triple: rdf.Triple{
			Subject: rdf.IRI("http://a.example/s-"),
			Predicate: rdf.IRI("http://a.example/p"),
			Object: rdf.IRI("http://a.example/o"),
		},
		TextOffsets: encoding.StatementTextOffsets{
			encoding.SubjectStatementOffsets: cursorio.TextOffsetRange{
				From: cursorio.TextOffset{Byte: 32, LineColumn: cursorio.TextLineColumn{1, 0}},
				Until: cursorio.TextOffset{Byte: 36, LineColumn: cursorio.TextLineColumn{1, 4}},
			},
			encoding.PredicateStatementOffsets: cursorio.TextOffsetRange{
				From: cursorio.TextOffset{Byte: 37, LineColumn: cursorio.TextLineColumn{1, 5}},
				Until: cursorio.TextOffset{Byte: 57, LineColumn: cursorio.TextLineColumn{1, 25}},
			},
			encoding.ObjectStatementOffsets: cursorio.TextOffsetRange{
				From: cursorio.TextOffset{Byte: 58, LineColumn: cursorio.TextLineColumn{1, 26}},
				Until: cursorio.TextOffset{Byte: 78, LineColumn: cursorio.TextLineColumn{1, 46}},
			},
		},
	},
}
